%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%
%%\tagged{Cat@One, Cat@Two, Cat@Three, Cat@Four, Cat@Five, Ans@MultiAns, Type@Concept, Topic@Derivative, Sub@Theorems_EVT}{

\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Does the Extreme Value Theorem hold for the function \[f(x)=\left\{\begin{array}{ll}
{\log\left(-x + 10\right)}\; , & x<{9}\\[3pt]
{\frac{1}{{\left(x - 8\right)}^{2}}}\; , & x\geq{9}
\end{array}\right.\]
 over the interval $[{5},{11}]$?

\input{2311_Concept_Derivative_0003.HELP.tex}
 
 \begin{multipleChoice}
 \choice{Yes}
 \choice[correct]{No}
 \end{multipleChoice}

If not, which condition fails?

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice[correct]{$f$ is not continuous on the interval}
\choice{The interval is not closed}
\choice{$f$ is not differentiable on the interval}
\choice{Nothing fails; the theorem holds}
\end{multipleChoice}
\end{problem}}%}
%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

{\log\left(-x + 10\right)}\; , & x<{9}\\[3pt]
{\frac{1}{{\left(x - 8\right)}^{9}}}\; , & x\geq{9}
\end{array}\right.\]
 over the interval $[{-11},{12}]$?

\input{2311_Concept_Derivative_0003.HELP.tex}
 
 \begin{multipleChoice}
 \choice{Yes}
 \choice[correct]{No}
 \end{multipleChoice}

If not, which condition fails?

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice[correct]{$f$ is not continuous on the interval}
\choice{The interval is not closed}
\choice{$f$ is not differentiable on the interval}
\choice{Nothing fails; the theorem holds}
\end{multipleChoice}
\end{problem}}{
%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%



}

Does the Extreme Value Theorem hold for the function \[f(x)=\left\{\begin{array}{ll}
{\log\left(-x - 3\right)}\; , & x<{-4}\\[3pt]
{\frac{1}{{\left(x + 5\right)}^{2}}}\; , & x\geq{-4}
\end{array}\right.\]
 over the interval $[{-19},{12}]$?

\input{2311_Concept_Derivative_0003.HELP.tex}
 
 \begin{multipleChoice}
 \choice{Yes}
 \choice[correct]{No}
 \end{multipleChoice}

If not, which condition fails?

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice[correct]{$f$ is not continuous on the interval}
\choice{The interval is not closed}
\choice{$f$ is not differentiable on the interval}
\choice{Nothing fails; the theorem holds}
\end{multipleChoice}
\end{problem}}{
%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%



}

\begin{problem}

Does the Extreme Value Theorem hold for the function \[f(x)=\left\{\begin{array}{ll}
{\log\left(-x + 6\right)}\; , & x<{5}\\[3pt]
{{\left(x - 4\right)}^{2}}\; , & x\geq{5}
\end{array}\right.\]
 over the interval $[{3},{18}]$?

\input{2311_Concept_Derivative_0003.HELP.tex}
 
 \begin{multipleChoice}
 \choice{Yes}
 \choice[correct]{No}
 \end{multipleChoice}

If not, which condition fails?

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice[correct]{$f$ is not continuous on the interval}
\choice{The interval is not closed}
\choice{$f$ is not differentiable on the interval}
\choice{Nothing fails; the theorem holds}
\end{multipleChoice}
\end{problem}}{
%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

\end{array}\right.\]

 \begin{multipleChoice}
 \choice{Yes}
 \choice[correct]{No}
 \end{multipleChoice}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice[correct]{$f$ is not continuous on the interval}
\choice{The interval is not closed}
\choice{$f$ is not differentiable on the interval}
\choice{Nothing fails; the theorem holds}
\end{multipleChoice}

Does the Extreme Value Theorem hold for the function \[f(x)=\left\{\begin{array}{ll}
{\log\left(-x - 4\right)}\; , & x<{-5}\\[3pt]
{\frac{1}{{\left(x + 6\right)}^{3}}}\; , & x\geq{-5}
\end{array}\right.\]
 over the interval $[{-20},{-3}]$?

\input{2311_Concept_Derivative_0003.HELP.tex}
 
 \begin{multipleChoice}
 \choice{Yes}
 \choice[correct]{No}
 \end{multipleChoice}

If not, which condition fails?

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice[correct]{$f$ is not continuous on the interval}
\choice{The interval is not closed}
\choice{$f$ is not differentiable on the interval}
\choice{Nothing fails; the theorem holds}
\end{multipleChoice}
\end{problem}}{
%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%



}

\choice{The interval is not closed}
\choice{$f$ is not differentiable on the interval}
\choice{Nothing fails; the theorem holds}
\end{multipleChoice}
\end{problem}}{
%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%



}
\latexProblemContent{
\begin{problem}

Does the Extreme Value Theorem hold for the function \[f(x)=\left\{\begin{array}{ll}
{\log\left(-x - 5\right)}\; , & x<{-6}\\[3pt]
{{\left(x + 7\right)}^{3}}\; , & x\geq{-6}
\end{array}\right.\]
 over the interval $[{-25},{11}]$?

\input{2311_Concept_Derivative_0003.HELP.tex}
 
 \begin{multipleChoice}
 \choice{Yes}
 \choice[correct]{No}
 \end{multipleChoice}

If not, which condition fails?

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice[correct]{$f$ is not continuous on the interval}
\choice{The interval is not closed}
\choice{$f$ is not differentiable on the interval}
\choice{Nothing fails; the theorem holds}
\end{multipleChoice}
\end{problem}}{
%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%



}
